0x00231e1f  ascii      coplanar ridges, concave ridges, and flipped facets.  In 4-d and higher,
0x00231e68  ascii      Qhull may produce a ridge with four neighbors or two facets with the same 
0x00231eb3  ascii      vertices.  Qhull reports these events when they occur.  It stops when a
0x00231efb  ascii      concave ridge, flipped facet, or duplicate facet occurs.
0x00231f3a  ascii      This is a Delaunay triangulation and the input is co-circular or co-spherical:
0x00231f89  ascii        - use 'Qz' to add a point "at infinity" (i.e., above the paraboloid)
0x00231fd0  ascii        - or use 'QJ' to joggle the input and avoid co-circular data
0x00232011  ascii      If the input is lower dimensional:
0x00232034  ascii        - use 'QJ' to joggle the input and make it full dimensional
0x00232072  ascii        - use 'Qbk:0Bk:0' to delete coordinate k from the input.  You should
0x002320b9  ascii          pick the coordinate with the least range.  The hull will have the
0x002320ff  ascii          correct topology.
0x00232115  ascii        - determine the flat containing the points, rotate the points
0x00232155  ascii          into a coordinate plane, and delete the other coordinates.
0x00232194  ascii        - add one or more points to make the input full dimensional.
0x002321d8  ascii        - recompile qhull for double precision (#define REALfloat 0 in qhull.h).
0x00232229  ascii      If the input should be full dimensional, you have several options that
0x00232270  ascii      may determine an initial simplex:
0x00232292  ascii        - use 'QJ'  to joggle the input and make it full dimensional
0x002322d1  ascii        - use 'QbB' to scale the points to the unit cube
0x00232304  ascii        - use 'QR0' to randomly rotate the input for different maximum points
0x0023234c  ascii        - use 'Qs'  to search all points for the initial simplex
0x00232387  ascii        - use 'En'  to specify a maximum roundoff error less than %2.2g.
0x002323ca  ascii        - trace execution with 'T3' to see the determinant for each point.
0x00232410  ascii        %d:  %8.4g  %8.4g  difference= %4.4g
0x00232439  ascii      The min and max coordinates for each dimension are:
0x00232471  ascii      Because of the high dimension, the min x-coordinate and max-coordinate
0x002324b8  ascii      points are used if the determinant is non-zero.  Option 'Qs' will
0x002324fa  ascii      do a better, though much slower, job.  Instead of 'Qs', you can change
0x00232541  ascii      the points by randomly rotating the input with 'QR0'.
0x00232579  ascii      These points either have a maximum or minimum x-coordinate, or
0x002325b8  ascii      they maximize the determinant for k coordinates.  Trial points
0x002325f7  ascii      are first selected from points that maximize a coordinate.
0x00232639  ascii      These points are the dual of the given halfspaces.  They indicate that
0x00232680  ascii      the intersection is degenerate.
